NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
I, T. Savithiri alias KT Savithiri, born on 17th June 1946 aged 68 years changed my name as
Tmt. R. SOMASUNDARAM through proceedings of the Superintendent Govt. R.M. Hospital, Thanjavur dated 28th July 1974.
I want to restore my old name as there are gender disparities. I also want my husband’s name as my initial. I, T. Savithiri
alias K.T Savithiri alias Tmt. R. Somasundaram will be henceforth called as SAVITHIRI, S.
Thanjavur,
27th April 2015.

Mrs. R. SOMASUNDARAM.

NOTICE BY COMPANY OF MEMBERS’ VOLUNTARY WINDING UP AND APPOINTMENT OF LIQUIDATOR.
At the Extraordinary General Meeting of the Company duly convened and held at its Registered Office on Friday, the
24th Day of April, 2015 the members have passed Special Resolution for:(i)

Voluntary winding up of the company under Section 484(1) (b) and other applicable Provisions, if any, of the Companies
Act, 1956 and for appointment of Mrs. Muthulakshmi Ganesh, Director of the Company, as the Liquidator in terms of
Section 490 and other applicable provisions, if any, of the Companies Act, 1956 and for fixing his remuneration,

(ii)

Authorizing the Liquidator to do all such acts and deeds as may be necessary for winding up the affairs of the company
and distributing its assets.

Dated at Chennai the 24th Day of April, 2015.

For HSR Investments Private Limited,
Urmila Aiyappan,
Director.

Chennai,
30th April 2015.

Form No. 155
[See Rule 329]
Members Winding Up
NAME OF THE COMPANY: ROSE AVIATION LIMITED
Notice convening Final Meeting
Notice is hereby given in pursuance of Section 497 of the Companies Act, 1956, that a General Meeting of the Members
of the above named Company will be held on Friday 26th June, 2015, at 443, Anna Salai, Teynampet, Chennai-600 018
at 10.00 A.M. for the purpose of having an account laid before the members showing them the manner in which the winding
up has been conducted and the property of the company disposed of and of hearing any explanation that may be given by
the liquidator and also of determining by a special resolution of the company, the manner in which the books, accounts and
documents of the company and of the liquidator shall be disposed of.
Chennai-18.
30th April 2015.

R. ALAGAR,
Liquidator.
